[b].[LogoUrl], [b].[Name], [b].[RowVersion], [b].[Slug], [b].[UpdatedAtUtc], [b].[UpdatedBy], [p0].[Id], [p0].[CreatedAtUtc], [p0].[CreatedBy], [p0].[DeletedAtUtc], [p0].[DeletedBy], [p0].[DisplayOrder], [p0].[IsDeleted], [p0].[IsPrimary], [p0].[ProductId], [p0].[PublicId], [p0].[RowVersion], [p0].[UpdatedAtUtc], [p0].[UpdatedBy], [p0].[Url], [p1].[Id], [p1].[Barcode], [p1].[CreatedAtUtc], [p1].[CreatedBy], [p1].[DeletedAtUtc], [p1].[DeletedBy], [p1].[ImagePublicId], [p1].[ImageUrl], [p1].[IsActive], [p1].[IsDeleted], [p1].[Name], [p1].[Price], [p1].[ProductId], [p1].[RowVersion], [p1].[Sku], [p1].[StockQuantity], [p1].[UpdatedAtUtc], [p1].[UpdatedBy]
FROM (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[Barcode], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CostPrice], [p].[CreatedAtUtc], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[DeletedAtUtc], [p].[DeletedBy], [p].[Description], [p].[DiscountEndDate], [p].[DiscountStartDate], [p].[DiscountType], [p].[DiscountValue], [p].[Height], [p].[IsActive], [p].[IsBestSeller], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFeatured], [p].[IsNewArrival], [p].[IsPublished], [p].[Length], [p].[MaximumStock], [p].[MetaDescription], [p].[MetaKeywords], [p].[MetaTitle], [p].[MinimumStock], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[RowVersion], [p].[ShortDescription], [p].[Sku], [p].[Slug], [p].[StockQuantity], [p].[StockStatus], [p].[SubCategoryId], [p].[TaxPercentage], [p].[UpdatedAtUtc], [p].[UpdatedBy], [p].[Weight], [p].[Width]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = @__isDeleted_Value_0 AND ([p].[CategoryId] = @__categoryId_Value_1 OR [p].[SubCategoryId] = @__categoryId_Value_2) AND [p].[StockStatus] = @__stockStatus_3 AND [p].[IsActive] = @__isActive_Value_4 AND [p].[IsPublished] = @__isPublished_Value_5
    ORDER BY [p].[CreatedAtUtc] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_6 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_7 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [t].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [Categories] AS [c0] ON [t].[SubCategoryId] = [c0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [Brands] AS [b] ON [t].[BrandId] = [b].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [ProductImages] AS [p0] ON [t].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN [ProductVariants] AS [p1] ON [t].[Id] = [p1].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [t].[CreatedAtUtc] DESC, [t].[Id], [c].[Id], [c0].[Id], [b].[Id], [p0].[Id]
